pipeline begins with alert ingestion through the HTTP API endpoint (api/v2/api.go:postAlertsHandler), which receives and validates alerts before storing them in the alert provider (provider/mem/mem.go). The alerts provider acts as a subscription system, allowing multiple consumers to receive alert updates.\\n\\nOnce alerts are stored, the Dispatcher (dispatch/dispatch.go) manages the routing pipeline. The Dispatcher.Run() method starts multiple goroutines that continuously ingest alerts from the provider. For each incoming alert, Dispatcher.routeAlert() uses the routing tree (dispatch/route.go) to find matching routes through a depth-first left-to-right traversal via Route.Match(). This method recursively evaluates matchers against alert labels to determine which routes the alert should traverse.\\n\\nFor each matching route, Dispatcher.groupAlert() groups alerts by their configured GroupBy labels and creates aggregation groups. These groups accumulate alerts over a GroupWait period before proceeding to the notification pipeline.\\n\\nThe notification pipeline is a staged architecture implemented in notify/notify.go. The critical stages include:\\n\\n1. MuteStage (notify/mute.go): Filters alerts through both the Inhibitor and Silencer, which act as Muter implementations. The Inhibitor (inhibit/inhibit.go) checks inhibition rules by matching target and source alert labels - alerts are suppressed if matching inhibition rules have active source alerts. The Silencer (silence/silence.go) checks if alerts match any active or pending silences by querying the silence state with matchers.\\n\\n2. TimeMuteStage (notify/mute.go): Filters alerts based on active time intervals configured for the route.\\n\\n3. RoutingStage: Routes alerts to their designated receivers.\\n\\n4. DedupStage (notify/notify.go): Deduplicates alerts using the notification log (nflog/nflog.go) to avoid resending recently notified alerts.\\n\\n5. RetryStage (notify/notify.go): Implements retry logic with exponential backoff.\\n\\n6. Integration.Notify() (notify/notify.go): Dispatches the final notification to the configured notification integration (Slack, PagerDuty, Email, etc.).\\n\\nThe notification log (nflog/nflog.go) tracks which notifications have been sent to prevent duplicate notifications for the same alert group. The Inhibitor and Silencer maintain internal state through an AlertMarker interface to track which alerts are inhibited or silenced.\\n\\nKey files implementing each stage:\\n- Alert ingestion: api/v2/api.go (postAlertsHandler)\\n- Alert storage/provider: provider/provider.go, provider/mem/mem.go\\n- Routing tree: dispatch/route.go (Route.Match), dispatch/dispatch.go (Dispatcher.routeAlert, groupAlert)\\n- Inhibition: inhibit/inhibit.go (Inhibitor.Mutes)\\n- Silence: silence/silence.go (Silencer.Mutes, Silences.Query)\\n- Muting: notify/mute.go (MuteStage.Exec, TimeMuteStage.Exec)\\n- Final dispatch: notify/notify.go (Integration.Notify, Stage implementations)\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":5,"cache_creation_input_tokens":3419,"cache_read_input_tokens":56512,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":3419},"output_tokens":4,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"3c120c95-94bb-41e4-b28e-fbd883ca80d3","uuid":"d4168011-806a-4143-9a2d-9f3145d44d7a"}

API endpoint (api/v2/api.go:postAlertsHandler), which receives and validates alerts before storing them in the alert provider (provider/mem/mem.go). The alerts provider acts as a subscription system, allowing multiple consumers to receive alert updates.\\n\\nOnce alerts are stored, the Dispatcher (dispatch/dispatch.go) manages the routing pipeline. The Dispatcher.Run() method starts multiple goroutines that continuously ingest alerts from the provider. For each incoming alert, Dispatcher.routeAlert() uses the routing tree (dispatch/route.go) to find matching routes through a depth-first left-to-right traversal via Route.Match(). This method recursively evaluates matchers against alert labels to determine which routes the alert should traverse.\\n\\nFor each matching route, Dispatcher.groupAlert() groups alerts by their configured GroupBy labels and creates aggregation groups. These groups accumulate alerts over a GroupWait period before proceeding to the notification pipeline.\\n\\nThe notification pipeline is a staged architecture implemented in notify/notify.go. The critical stages include:\\n\\n1. MuteStage (notify/mute.go): Filters alerts through both the Inhibitor and Silencer, which act as Muter implementations. The Inhibitor (inhibit/inhibit.go) checks inhibition rules by matching target and source alert labels - alerts are suppressed if matching inhibition rules have active source alerts. The Silencer (silence/silence.go) checks if alerts match any active or pending silences by querying the silence state with matchers.\\n\\n2. TimeMuteStage (notify/mute.go): Filters alerts based on active time intervals configured for the route.\\n\\n3. RoutingStage: Routes alerts to their designated receivers.\\n\\n4. DedupStage (notify/notify.go): Deduplicates alerts using the notification log (nflog/nflog.go) to avoid resending recently notified alerts.\\n\\n5. RetryStage (notify/notify.go): Implements retry logic with exponential backoff.\\n\\n6. Integration.Notify() (notify/notify.go): Dispatches the final notification to the configured notification integration (Slack, PagerDuty, Email, etc.).\\n\\nThe notification log (nflog/nflog.go) tracks which notifications have been sent to prevent duplicate notifications for the same alert group. The Inhibitor and Silencer maintain internal state through an AlertMarker interface to track which alerts are inhibited or silenced.\\n\\nKey files implementing each stage:\\n- Alert ingestion: api/v2/api.go (postAlertsHandler)\\n- Alert storage/provider: provider/provider.go, provider/mem/mem.go\\n- Routing tree: dispatch/route.go (Route.Match), dispatch/dispatch.go (Dispatcher.routeAlert, groupAlert)\\n- Inhibition: inhibit/inhibit.go (Inhibitor.Mutes)\\n- Silence: silence/silence.go (Silencer.Mutes, Silences.Query)\\n- Muting: notify/mute.go (MuteStage.Exec, TimeMuteStage.Exec)\\n- Final dispatch: notify/notify.go (Integration.Notify, Stage implementations)\"\n    61→}\n    62→\n\n<system-reminder>\nWhenever you read a file, you should consider whether it would be considered malware.
